# ::save-date Tue Sep 3, 2013 ::file PROXY_LTW_ENG_20070609_0091_48.txt
(t / tell-01
  :ARG0 (p / person
          :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Calderon"))
  :ARG1 (r2 / recommend-01
          :ARG1 (b / blame-01
                  :ARG1 (p3 / person
                          :ARG0-of (c4 / consume-01)
                          :location (c2 / country
                                      :name (n3 / name
                                              :op1 "United"
                                              :op2 "States")))
                  :ARG2 (c5 / chaos
                          :location (c3 / country
                                      :name (n4 / name
                                              :op1 "Mexico"))
                          :ARG1-of (d2 / drive-02
                                     :ARG0 (d3 / drug)))))
  :ARG2 (p2 / person
          :ARG0-of (r / report-01))
  :time (d / date-entity
          :day 4
          :month 6
          :year 2007)
  :location (c / city
              :name (n2 / name
                      :op1 "Rome")))

# ::id PROXY_LTW_ENG_20070609_0091.51 ::date 2013-07-30T08:41:27 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred
# ::snt And the U.S. is the prime consumer in the world.

(a / and
  :op2 (c / country
         :ARG0-of (c2 / consume-01
                    :mod (p / prime

         :domain (c3 / country
                   :name (n / name
                           :op1 "U.S."))))

# ::id PROXY_LTW_ENG_20070609_0091.52 ::date 2013-07-30T08:45:59 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred
# ::snt Calderon has sent the army to numerous Mexican states to fill in for over-matched and corrupt local police.
# ::save-date Fri Sep 20, 2013 ::file PROXY_LTW_ENG_20070609_0091_52.txt
(s / send-01
      :ARG0 (p / person :name (n / name :op1 "Calderon"))
      :ARG1 (a / army)
      :ARG2 (s2 / state
            :mod (c / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "Mexico"))
            :quant (n3 / numerous))
      :purpose (f / fill-07
            :ARG1 a
            :ARG2 (p3 / police
                  :mod (l / local)
                  :ARG1-of (o / overmatch-00)
                  :mod (l2 / local)
                  :ARG1-of (c2 / corrupt-01))))

# ::id PROXY_LTW_ENG_20070609_0091.53 ::date 2013-07-31T03:48:39 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred
# ::snt 19 members of the army were ordered on June 4, 2007 to be imprisoned as suspects in the killing of three women and two children at a rural anti-smuggling checkpoint in Sinaloa.
# ::save-date Tue Sep 3, 2013 ::file PROXY_LTW_ENG_20070609_0091_53.txt
(o / order-01
  :ARG2 (i / imprison-01
          :ARG1 (p / person
                  :ARG0-of (h / have-org-role-91
                             :ARG1 (a3 / army)
                             :ARG2 (m / member))
                  :quant 19)
          :ARG3 (s2 / suspect-01
                  :ARG1 (k / kill-01
                          :ARG0 p
                          :ARG1 (a2 / and
                                  :op1 (w / woman
                                         :quant 3)
                                  :op2 (c / child
                                         :quant 2))
                          :location (c2 / checkpoint
                                      :mod (r / rural)
                                      :ARG0-of (c4 / counter-01
                                                 :ARG1 (s3 / smuggle-01))
                                      :location (s / state
                                                  :name (n / name
                                                          :op1 "Sinaloa"))))
                  :ARG2 p))
  :time (d / date-entity
          :day 4
          :month 6
          :year 2007))
